> 2>&1 is the explicit redirection operator:

> It means â€œsend file descriptor 2 (stderr) to wherever file descriptor 1 (stdout) is currently going.â€ ^ref-b3555ede-4-0

> Works in all POSIX shells (sh, bash, zsh, dash, etc.). ^ref-b3555ede-6-0
```mermaid
flowchart LR
command --> stdout
command --> stderr
stdout --> file
stderr --> file
```
^ref-b3555ede-7-0
 ^ref-b3555ede-15-0
> &> is a bash/zsh shorthand:
 ^ref-b3555ede-17-0
> It means â€œredirect both stdout and stderr to the same target.â€
 ^ref-b3555ede-19-0
> Not POSIX; wonâ€™t work in plain sh or some other shells.
 ^ref-b3555ede-21-0
